        conteudo = React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 12 } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 13, color: C.mute, lineHeight: 1.5, marginBottom: 2 } }, "Sem ideias? Deixa com a gente. Escolha como quer criar:"),
            React.createElement("button", { onClick: dispararRapida, style: { width: "100%", padding: "18px 16px", borderRadius: 14, border: "none", background: "linear-gradient(135deg, ".concat(C.amber, ", ").concat(C.amberDeep, ")"), color: "var(--onAccent)", fontFamily: "'DM Sans',sans-serif", cursor: "pointer", textAlign: "left", boxShadow: "0 8px 24px rgba(179,102,255,.3)" } },
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 17, fontWeight: 800, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8 } }, "\u26A1 Gera\u00E7\u00E3o R\u00E1pida"),
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 12.5, opacity: .92, marginTop: 4, fontWeight: 500, lineHeight: 1.45 } }, "Um clique e pronto. A IA usa seu perfil e cria uma pauta completa \u2014 sem perguntas.")),
            React.createElement("button", { onClick: function () { return setFase("personalizada"); }, style: { width: "100%", padding: "16px", borderRadius: 14, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: C.soft, color: C.ink, fontFamily: "'DM Sans',sans-serif", cursor: "pointer", textAlign: "left" } },
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 700, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8 } }, "\uD83C\uDFAF Gera\u00E7\u00E3o Personalizada"),
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 12.5, color: C.mute, marginTop: 4, lineHeight: 1.45 } }, "Quer dar dire\u00E7\u00F5es? Informe tema, produto ou objetivo \u2014 tudo opcional.")));
    }
    return React.createElement(React.Fragment, null,
        React.createElement("div", { onClick: fase === "loading" ? null : onFechar, style: { position: "fixed", inset: 0, background: "rgba(0,0,0,.65)", zIndex: 500, backdropFilter: "blur(2px)" } }),
        React.createElement("div", { className: "modal-center", style: { position: "fixed", left: "50%", top: "50%", transform: "translate(-50%,-50%)", width: "min(400px, calc(100vw - 24px))", maxHeight: "88vh", overflowY: "auto", zIndex: 501, background: C.card, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), borderRadius: 18, padding: "0 0 20px", boxShadow: "0 24px 60px rgba(0,0,0,.7)" } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "16px 18px 12px", borderBottom: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), position: "sticky", top: 0, background: C.card, zIndex: 1, display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "center", borderRadius: "18px 18px 0 0" } },
                React.createElement("div", null,
                    React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 11, color: C.mute, fontWeight: 600, textTransform: "uppercase", letterSpacing: 1 } }, "Pauta para"),
                    React.createElement("div", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 800, color: C.ink } }, dataLabel)),
                fase !== "loading" && React.createElement("button", { onClick: onFechar, style: { background: C.soft, border: "none", color: C.mute, fontSize: 18, cursor: "pointer", width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: "50%", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", lineHeight: 1 } }, "\u00D7")),
            React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "16px 18px 0" } }, conteudo)));
}

// Microcopy: gera um comentário curto e inteligente sobre a pauta recém-criada.
// Em vez de a pauta só "aparecer", o app COMENTA com base no conteúdo real —
// isso humaniza o produto (deixa de ser máquina que cospe resultado).
function comentarioPauta(posts, nicho) {
    if (!Array.isArray(posts) || posts.length === 0) return null;
    var formatos = posts.map(function (p) { return (p.formato || "").toLowerCase(); });
    var temReels = formatos.some(function (f) { return f.indexOf("reels") >= 0 || f.indexOf("v\u00EDdeo") >= 0 || f.indexOf("video") >= 0; });
    var temStory = formatos.some(function (f) { return f.indexOf("story") >= 0 || f.indexOf("stories") >= 0; });
    var qtd = posts.length;
    if (temReels && qtd >= 3) return "\uD83D\uDD25 Pauta forte hoje \u2014 tem Reels com bom potencial de alcance. Capriche no gancho dos 3 primeiros segundos!";
    if (temReels) return "\u2728 Boa! Reels costuma alcan\u00E7ar mais gente nova. O gancho inicial \u00E9 o que segura o espectador.";
    if (temStory && qtd >= 3) return "\uD83D\uDCAC Dia de conex\u00E3o: v\u00E1rios Stories ajudam a aproximar sua audi\u00EAncia e manter presen\u00E7a.";
    if (nicho) return "\uD83C\uDFAF Pauta pensada pro seu nicho de " + nicho + ". Consist\u00EAncia \u00E9 o que faz crescer!";
    return "\u2728 Pauta pronta! Consist\u00EAncia \u00E9 o que faz o algoritmo (e a audi\u00EAncia) confiar em voc\u00EA.";
}
function DiaConteudo(_a) {
    var dia = _a.dia, estado = _a.estado, onGerar = _a.onGerar, desempenho = _a.desempenho, onRate = _a.onRate, onUpgrade = _a.onUpgrade, produtosAfiliar = _a.produtosAfiliar, onPromover = _a.onPromover, nichoCriador = _a.nichoCriador, dataDoDia = _a.dataDoDia, producao = _a.producao, onProduzir = _a.onProduzir, planoNivel = _a.planoNivel, checklist = _a.checklist, onChecklistItem = _a.onChecklistItem, onMelhora = _a.onMelhora, planejado = _a.planejado, onEditarPlanejado = _a.onEditarPlanejado, diaPassou = _a.diaPassou, onCancelar = _a.onCancelar;
    var LOAD_MSGS = ["\uD83E\uDDE0 Analisando seu perfil...", "\uD83D\uDCA1 Pensando nos melhores conte\u00FAdos...", "\u270D\uFE0F Escrevendo os roteiros...", "\uD83C\uDFAC Montando o passo a passo de grava\u00E7\u00E3o...", "\u2728 Finalizando sua pauta exclusiva..."];
    var _lm = __read(React.useState(0), 2), loadMsg = _lm[0], setLoadMsg = _lm[1];
    var estaCarregando = !!(estado && estado.loading);
    React.useEffect(function () {
        if (!estaCarregando) { setLoadMsg(0); return; }
        var iv = setInterval(function () { setLoadMsg(function (i) { return Math.min(i + 1, LOAD_MSGS.length - 1); }); }, 2600);
        return function () { return clearInterval(iv); };
    }, [estaCarregando]);
    function agendarLembrete(post) {
        try {
            var horarioStr = (post.melhor_horario || "19h").replace(/[^0-9:h]/gi, "");
            var hora = parseInt(horarioStr, 10);
            if (isNaN(hora)) hora = 19;
            var min = 0;
            if (horarioStr.indexOf(":") >= 0) { var pm = horarioStr.split(":"); hora = parseInt(pm[0], 10); min = parseInt(pm[1], 10) || 0; }
            var base = dataDoDia ? new Date(dataDoDia + "T00:00:00") : new Date();
            base.setHours(hora, min, 0, 0);
            // se a data/hora já passou hoje, joga pra daqui a pouco
            if (base.getTime() < Date.now()) { base = new Date(Date.now() + 3600000); }
            var fim = new Date(base.getTime() + 30 * 60000);
            function fmt(d) {
                function p(n) { return n < 10 ? "0" + n : "" + n; }
                return d.getFullYear() + p(d.getMonth() + 1) + p(d.getDate()) + "T" + p(d.getHours()) + p(d.getMinutes()) + "00";
            }
            var titulo = "Postar: " + (post.tema || "conteúdo") + " (" + (post.formato || "post") + ")";
            var desc = (post.gancho ? "Gancho: " + post.gancho + "\\n" : "") + (post.cta ? "CTA: " + post.cta : "");
            var ics = ["BEGIN:VCALENDAR", "VERSION:2.0", "PRODID:-//Cria//PT", "BEGIN:VEVENT", "UID:" + Date.now() + "@cria", "DTSTAMP:" + fmt(new Date()), "DTSTART:" + fmt(base), "DTEND:" + fmt(fim), "SUMMARY:" + titulo, "DESCRIPTION:" + desc, "BEGIN:VALARM", "TRIGGER:-PT15M", "ACTION:DISPLAY", "DESCRIPTION:Hora de postar no Cria", "END:VALARM", "END:VEVENT", "END:VCALENDAR"].join("\r\n");
            var blob = new Blob([ics], { type: "text/calendar;charset=utf-8" });
            var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
            var a = document.createElement("a");
            a.href = url; a.download = "lembrete-cria.ics";
            document.body.appendChild(a); a.click();
            document.body.removeChild(a);
            setTimeout(function () { URL.revokeObjectURL(url); }, 1000);
        } catch (e) { try { toastErro("Não consegui criar o lembrete neste aparelho."); } catch (e2) { } }
    }
    if (!estado) {
        if (diaPassou) {
            return React.createElement(EstadoVazio, { emoji: "\uD83D\uDCC5", titulo: "Este dia j\u00E1 passou", texto: "N\u00E3o \u00E9 poss\u00EDvel gerar pauta para uma data anterior. Selecione hoje ou um dia futuro." });
        }
        return React.createElement(EstadoVazio, {
            emoji: "\u2728",
            titulo: "Nenhuma pauta ainda",
            texto: "Toque no bot\u00E3o e a IA cria a pauta completa de " + dia + " pra voc\u00EA.",
            acao: React.createElement(Botao, { onClick: onGerar, full: false, style: { maxWidth: 260 } }, "\u26A1 Gerar pauta de " + dia)
        });
    }
    if (estado.loading) {
        return React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "8px 0" } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10, marginBottom: DS.sp.md } },
                React.createElement("div", { style: { width: 24, height: 24, border: "3px solid ".concat(C.line), borderTopColor: C.amber, borderRadius: "50%", animation: "spin .9s linear infinite", flexShrink: 0 } }),
                React.createElement("p", { style: { color: C.amber, fontWeight: DS.fw.bold, margin: 0, flex: 1, fontSize: 14 } }, LOAD_MSGS[loadMsg])),
            React.createElement(Skeleton, { h: 14, w: "40%", mb: DS.sp.md }),
            React.createElement(Skeleton, { h: 60, mb: DS.sp.md }),
            React.createElement(Skeleton, { h: 14, w: "70%" }),
            React.createElement(Skeleton, { h: 14, w: "55%" }),
            React.createElement(Skeleton, { h: 40, mb: DS.sp.md }),
            onCancelar && React.createElement("button", { onClick: onCancelar, style: { width: "100%", padding: "12px", borderRadius: DS.r.md, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: "transparent", color: C.mute, fontFamily: DS.ff.body, fontSize: 13.5, fontWeight: DS.fw.bold, cursor: "pointer" } }, "Cancelar geração"),
            React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 11.5, color: C.mute, textAlign: "center", marginTop: 10, lineHeight: 1.5 } }, "Pautas completas com roteiro e passo a passo levam alguns segundos. Vale a pena! \u2728"));
    }
    if (estado.erro === "RATE_LIMIT") {
        return (React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: 18, borderRadius: 14, background: "rgba(255,180,0,.08)", border: "1px solid rgba(255,180,0,.35)", textAlign: "center" } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 30 } }, "\u23F3"),
            React.createElement("strong", { className: "disp", style: { display: "block", fontSize: 16, marginTop: 6 } }, "Muitas gera\u00E7\u00F5es simult\u00E2neas"),
            React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 13, color: C.mute, margin: "8px 0 14px", lineHeight: 1.5 } }, "O servi\u00E7o atingiu o limite de uso por hora. Aguarde alguns minutos e tente de novo \u2014 seus outros dias n\u00E3o s\u00E3o afetados."),
            React.createElement(Botao, { onClick: onGerar, style: { maxWidth: 220, marginLeft: "auto", marginRight: "auto" } }, "Tentar de novo")));
    }
    if (estado.erro === "LIMITE") {
        return (React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: 18, borderRadius: 14, background: "rgba(179,102,255,.1)", border: "1px solid rgba(179,102,255,.4)", textAlign: "center" } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 30 } }, "\uD83D\uDD12"),
            React.createElement("strong", { className: "disp", style: { display: "block", fontSize: 17, marginTop: 6 } }, "Voc\u00EA usou todas as pautas da semana"),
            React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 13, color: C.mute, margin: "8px 0 0", lineHeight: 1.5 } }, "Seu limite zera no pr\u00F3ximo domingo. Pra gerar mais agora, fa\u00E7a upgrade do plano."),
            onUpgrade && React.createElement(Botao, { onClick: onUpgrade, style: { marginTop: 14, maxWidth: 220, marginLeft: "auto", marginRight: "auto" } }, "Ver planos")));
    }
    if (estado.erro) {
        var ehDiaPassado = diaPassou;
        if (ehDiaPassado || (estado.erro && estado.erro.includes("já passou"))) {
            return (React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "18px 16px", borderRadius: 12, background: C.soft, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), textAlign: "center" } },
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 28, marginBottom: 8 } }, "\uD83D\uDCC5"),
                React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 14, color: C.mute, lineHeight: 1.5, margin: 0 } },
                    "Este dia já passou.",
                    React.createElement("br", null),
                    React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 12.5 } }, "Selecione hoje ou um dia futuro para gerar pautas."))));
        }
        return (React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: 14, borderRadius: 12, background: "#2a1414", border: "1px solid #4a2020" } },
            React.createElement("strong", { style: { color: C.rose } }, "Opa."),
            React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 12.5, color: "#ffb3b3", margin: "8px 0 0", wordBreak: "break-word" } }, estado.erro),
            React.createElement(Botao, { onClick: onGerar, style: { marginTop: 14 } }, "Tentar de novo")));
    }
    var _c = estado.data || {}, foco_do_dia = _c.foco_do_dia, posts = _c.posts;
    if (!Array.isArray(posts)) posts = [];
    // Se não há dados nem posts, trata como estado vazio (não quebra a tela).
    if (!estado.gerandoParcial && (!estado.data || (posts.length === 0 && !foco_do_dia))) {
        return React.createElement(EstadoVazio, { emoji: "\u2728", titulo: "Nenhuma pauta ainda", texto: "Toque no bot\u00E3o e a IA cria a pauta completa de " + dia + " pra voc\u00EA.", acao: !diaPassou && React.createElement(Botao, { onClick: onGerar, full: false, style: { maxWidth: 260 } }, "\u26A1 Gerar pauta de " + dia) });
    }
    var dicaProduto = (function () {
        var lista = (produtosAfiliar || []).filter(function (p) { return p && p.temAfiliados !== false && p.ativo !== false && !p.privado; });
        if (lista.length === 0) return null;
        // Filtra por relevância com o nicho do criador
        var nicho = (nichoCriador || "").toLowerCase().trim();
        if (nicho) {
            var palavrasNicho = nicho.split(/[\s,\/]+/).filter(function (w) { return w.length > 2; });
            var relevantes = lista.filter(function (p) {
                var alvo = ((p.categoria || "") + " " + (p.nome || "") + " " + (p.descricao || "")).toLowerCase();
                if (alvo.indexOf(nicho) >= 0) return true;
                return palavrasNicho.some(function (w) { return alvo.indexOf(w) >= 0; });
            });
            // Se houver produtos relevantes, usa só eles; senão, não mostra dica
            if (relevantes.length > 0) lista = relevantes;
            else return null;
        }
        // Mostra ocasionalmente (~40% das pautas), de forma consistente pra mesma pauta
        var seed = ((foco_do_dia || "") + (posts && posts.length ? posts[0].tema || "" : "")).length;
        if (seed % 5 >= 2) return null;
        return lista[seed % lista.length];
    })();
    return (React.createElement("div", { className: "rise" },
        dicaProduto && React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "13px 15px", borderRadius: 14, marginBottom: 16, background: "linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(62,224,163,.12), rgba(179,102,255,.08))", border: "1px solid rgba(62,224,163,.35)" } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 10.5, letterSpacing: 1, color: C.green, textTransform: "uppercase", fontWeight: 700, marginBottom: 4 } }, "💡 Oportunidade de renda"),
            React.createElement("p", { style: { margin: "0 0 4px", fontSize: 13.5, color: C.ink, lineHeight: 1.5 } },
                "Que tal divulgar ", React.createElement("strong", null, dicaProduto.nome), " no seu conteúdo de hoje? Você ganha ", React.createElement("strong", { style: { color: C.green } }, (dicaProduto.comissao || 30) + "% de comissão"), " por venda."),
            React.createElement("button", { onClick: function () { return onPromover && onPromover(dicaProduto); }, style: { marginTop: 6, padding: "8px 14px", borderRadius: 9, border: "none", cursor: "pointer", fontFamily: "'DM Sans',sans-serif", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: 12.5, background: "linear-gradient(135deg, var(--accent), var(--rose))", color: "var(--onAccent)" } }, "🔗 Quero promover este produto")),
        planejado && React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "11px 14px", borderRadius: 12, marginBottom: 12, background: "rgba(62,224,163,.07)", border: "1px solid rgba(62,224,163,.25)", display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "flex-start", gap: 10 } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { minWidth: 0 } },
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 10.5, color: C.green, fontWeight: 700, textTransform: "uppercase", letterSpacing: .5, marginBottom: 3 } }, "\uD83D\uDCCC Planejamento salvo"),
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 13.5, fontWeight: 700, color: C.ink, whiteSpace: "nowrap", overflow: "hidden", textOverflow: "ellipsis" } }, planejado.titulo),
                (planejado.plataforma || planejado.formato) && React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 11.5, color: C.mute, marginTop: 3 } }, [planejado.plataforma, planejado.formato].filter(Boolean).join(" · "))),
            onEditarPlanejado && React.createElement("button", { onClick: onEditarPlanejado, style: { flexShrink: 0, background: "transparent", border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), borderRadius: 8, color: C.mute, fontFamily: "'DM Sans',sans-serif", fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, padding: "4px 9px", cursor: "pointer" } }, "Editar")),
        foco_do_dia && (React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "12px 15px", borderRadius: 12, marginBottom: 16, background: "rgba(179,102,255,.08)", borderLeft: "3px solid ".concat(C.amber) } },
            React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 11, letterSpacing: 1.5, color: C.amber, textTransform: "uppercase" } },
                "Foco de ",
                dia),
            React.createElement("p", { style: { margin: "5px 0 0", fontSize: 14, lineHeight: 1.5 } }, foco_do_dia))),
        !diaPassou && (function () {
            var coment = comentarioPauta(posts, nichoCriador);
            return coment ? React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "10px 14px", borderRadius: 12, marginBottom: 16, background: "rgba(62,224,163,.07)", border: "1px solid rgba(62,224,163,.2)", fontSize: 13, color: C.ink, lineHeight: 1.5 } }, coment) : null;
        })(),
        estado.gerandoParcial && React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "12px 14px", borderRadius: 12, marginBottom: 14, background: "rgba(179,102,255,.06)", border: "1px solid rgba(179,102,255,.2)", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10 } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { width: 18, height: 18, border: "2px solid ".concat(C.line), borderTopColor: C.amber, borderRadius: "50%", animation: "spin .9s linear infinite", flexShrink: 0 } }),
            React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 12.5, color: C.amber, fontWeight: 700 } }, "Gerando os posts... " + (posts.length) + (estado.totalEsperado ? " de " + estado.totalEsperado : "") + " prontos"),
            onCancelar && React.createElement("button", { onClick: onCancelar, style: { marginLeft: "auto", padding: "5px 10px", borderRadius: 8, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: "transparent", color: C.mute, fontSize: 11.5, fontWeight: 700, cursor: "pointer", flexShrink: 0 } }, "Parar")),
        posts.map(function (post, i) {
            var roteiroTxt = roteiroTexto(post.roteiro);
            var cenas = storyboardCenas(post.storyboard);
            var totalSeg = duracaoTotal(post.storyboard);
            var keyProd = "".concat(dia, "|").concat(i);
            var statusProd = producao[keyProd];
            var chk = checklist[keyProd] || {};
            var temResultado = !!desempenho[keyProd];
            var etapaAtual = etapaDoPost(statusProd, chk, temResultado);
            return (React.createElement("div", { key: i, className: "rise", style: { animationDelay: "".concat(i * 0.07, "s"), marginBottom: 14, borderRadius: 16, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: C.card, overflow: "hidden" } },
                React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "14px 16px 0", display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "center", gap: 8 } },
                    React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 11, padding: "3px 10px", borderRadius: 20, background: "linear-gradient(135deg, ".concat(C.amber, ", ").concat(C.amberDeep, ")"), color: "var(--onAccent)", fontWeight: 700 } }, post.formato),
                    totalSeg && React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 12, color: C.mute, fontWeight: 600 } },
                        "\u23F1\uFE0F \u007E", totalSeg, "s")),
                React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "10px 16px 0" } },
                    React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", gap: 3, marginBottom: 5 } }, ETAPAS_PROD.map(function (et, idx) {
                        return React.createElement("div", { key: idx, style: { flex: 1, height: 4, borderRadius: 3, background: idx <= etapaAtual ? "linear-gradient(135deg, var(--accent), var(--rose))" : C.line } });
                    })),
                    React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 10.5, color: etapaAtual === 5 ? C.green : C.amber, fontWeight: 700 } }, ETAPAS_PROD[etapaAtual] + (etapaAtual < 5 ? " \u00B7 etapa " + (etapaAtual + 1) + " de 6" : " \uD83C\uDF89"))),
                React.createElement("div", { style: { padding: "8px 16px 16px" } },
                    post.promo_cria && React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "inline-block", marginBottom: 8, fontSize: 10.5, fontWeight: 700, color: C.green, background: "rgba(62,224,163,.12)", border: "1px solid rgba(62,224,163,.3)", borderRadius: 7, padding: "2px 9px" } }, "\uD83D\uDC9C Ideia que fala sobre o Cria"),
                    React.createElement(Rot, null, "\uD83D\uDCCC T\u00EDtulo"),
                    React.createElement("h3", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 19, margin: "3px 0 0", lineHeight: 1.2, fontWeight: 700 } }, post.tema),
                    React.createElement(Bloco, { rotulo: "\uD83E\uDE9D Gancho", texto: post.gancho, cor: C.amber }),
                    roteiroTxt && (React.createElement("div", { style: { marginTop: 12 } },
                        React.createElement(Rot, null, "\uD83C\uDFAC Roteiro"),
                        React.createElement("p", { style: { margin: "5px 0 0", fontSize: 13.5, lineHeight: 1.6, color: C.ink, whiteSpace: "pre-wrap" } }, roteiroTxt))),
                    cenas.length > 0 && (React.createElement("div", { style: { marginTop: 14 } },

function MarcasScreen(_a) {
    var profile = _a.profile, ofertas = _a.ofertas, setOfertas = _a.setOfertas, mensagens = _a.mensagens, addMsg = _a.addMsg;
    var _b = __read(React.useState(null), 2), chatAberto = _b[0], setChatAberto = _b[1];
    var brl = function (n) { return Number(n || 0).toLocaleString("pt-BR", { style: "currency", currency: "BRL" }); };
    var meus = profile.metricas || { seguidores: 0, alcance: 0, eng: 0 };
    var nichoMatch = function (of) {
        var a = (of.nicho || "").toLowerCase().trim();
        var b = (profile.nicho || "").toLowerCase().trim();
        return !!a && !!b && (a.includes(b) || b.includes(a));
    };
    var combina = function (of) { return nichoMatch(of) && (!of.seguidoresMin || meus.seguidores >= of.seguidoresMin) && (!of.alcanceMin || meus.alcance >= of.alcanceMin); };
    var compatibilidade = function (of) {
        var pontos = 0; var razoes = []; var total = 0;
        total += 40;
        if (nichoMatch(of)) { pontos += 40; razoes.push("Seu nicho combina com o que a marca procura"); }
        else { razoes.push("Seu nicho não é o foco desta campanha"); }
        total += 30;
        if (!of.seguidoresMin || meus.seguidores >= of.seguidoresMin) { pontos += 30; razoes.push("Sua audiência atende ao mínimo da campanha"); }
        else { razoes.push("A campanha pede " + (of.seguidoresMin || 0).toLocaleString("pt-BR") + " seguidores (você tem " + meus.seguidores.toLocaleString("pt-BR") + ")"); }
        total += 20;
        if (!of.alcanceMin || meus.alcance >= of.alcanceMin) { pontos += 20; razoes.push("Seu alcance médio está dentro do esperado"); }
        else { razoes.push("A campanha pede " + (of.alcanceMin || 0).toLocaleString("pt-BR") + " de alcance"); }
        total += 10;
        if (profile.verificado) { pontos += 10; razoes.push("Sua conta é verificada — marcas preferem criadores verificados"); }
        var pct = Math.round(pontos / total * 100);
        return { pct: pct, razoes: razoes };
    };
    function candidatar(of) {
        if (!profile.verificado)
            return;
        setOfertas(function (arr) { return arr.map(function (x) {
            if (x.id !== of.id)
                return x;
            if ((x.candidatos || []).some(function (c) { return c.nome === (profile.nome || "Criador"); }))
                return x;
            var cand = { nome: profile.nome || "Criador", nicho: profile.nicho, seguidores: meus.seguidores, alcance: meus.alcance, eng: meus.eng, publico: profile.publico, plataformas: profile.plataformas, portfolio: profile.portfolio, status: "pendente" };
            return __assign(__assign({}, x), { candidatos: __spreadArray(__spreadArray([], __read((x.candidatos || [])), false), [cand], false) });
        }); });
        notify && notify("marca", "Novo candidato: ".concat(profile.nome || "Criador", " se inscreveu em \"").concat(of.titulo, "\""));
    }
    function enviarEntrega(of) {
        setOfertas(function (arr) { return arr.map(function (x) { return x.id !== of.id ? x : __assign(__assign({}, x), { candidatos: x.candidatos.map(function (c) { return c.nome === (profile.nome || "Criador") ? __assign(__assign({}, c), { status: "entregue", entrega: "minha-entrega.mp4" }) : c; }) }); }); });
        notify && notify("marca", "".concat(profile.nome || "Criador", " enviou a entrega de \"").concat(of.titulo, "\""));
    }
    function avaliarMarca(of, n) {
        setOfertas(function (arr) { return arr.map(function (x) { return x.id !== of.id ? x : __assign(__assign({}, x), { candidatos: x.candidatos.map(function (c) { return c.nome === (profile.nome || "Criador") ? __assign(__assign({}, c), { notaMarca: n }) : c; }) }); }); });
    }
    function responderConvite(of, aceitar) {
        setOfertas(function (arr) { return arr.map(function (x) { return x.id !== of.id ? x : __assign(__assign({}, x), { candidatos: x.candidatos.map(function (c) { return c.nome === (profile.nome || "Criador") ? __assign(__assign({}, c), { status: aceitar ? "aprovado" : "recusado" }) : c; }) }); }); });
        notify && notify("marca", "".concat(profile.nome || "Criador", " ").concat(aceitar ? "aceitou" : "recusou", " o convite de \"").concat(of.titulo, "\""));
    }
    var reputacaoMarca = function (marca) { return mediaNota(ofertas.filter(function (o) { return o.marca === marca; }).flatMap(function (o) { return (o.candidatos || []).map(function (c) { return c.notaMarca || 0; }); })); };
    var ofertasVisiveis = ofertas.filter(function (o) { return o.status !== "aguardando_deposito"; });
    return (React.createElement("div", { className: "rise" },
        React.createElement("h2", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 24, margin: "16px 0 2px", fontWeight: 700 } }, "Vagas de marcas"),
        React.createElement(Sub, null, "Candidate-se \u00E0s campanhas das marcas. Os valores j\u00E1 s\u00E3o o que voc\u00EA recebe, limpo."),
        React.createElement("div", { style: { marginBottom: 14, padding: "11px 13px", borderRadius: 12, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: profile.verificado ? "rgba(126,224,138,.08)" : "rgba(255,107,107,.07)" } }, profile.verificado
            ? React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 12.5, margin: 0, color: C.green } },
                "\u2713 M\u00E9tricas verificadas: ",
                meus.seguidores.toLocaleString("pt-BR"),

                " alcance \u00B7 ",

            : React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 12.5, margin: 0, color: C.rose } }, "\u26A0 Conecte sua conta no Perfil pra verificar. Sem isso, voc\u00EA n\u00E3o pode se candidatar.")),
        ofertas.length === 0 ? React.createElement(EstadoVazio, { emoji: "\uD83D\uDCE2", titulo: "Nenhuma campanha ainda", texto: "Quando marcas publicarem campanhas do seu nicho, elas aparecem aqui com o quanto você pode ganhar." }) : __spreadArray([], __read(ofertas), false).sort(function (a, b) { return (combina(b) ? 1 : 0) - (combina(a) ? 1 : 0); }).map(function (of) {
            var meu = (of.candidatos || []).find(function (c) { return c.nome === (profile.nome || "Criador"); });
            var bateSeg = !of.seguidoresMin || meus.seguidores >= of.seguidoresMin;
            var bateAlc = !of.alcanceMin || meus.alcance >= of.alcanceMin;
            return (React.createElement("div", { key: of.id, style: { borderRadius: 14, border: "1px solid ".concat(combina(of) ? "rgba(126,224,138,.5)" : C.line), background: C.card, padding: 15, marginBottom: 12 } },
                (function () {
                    var compat = compatibilidade(of);
                    return React.createElement("div", { style: { marginBottom: 10 } },
                        React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, marginBottom: 6 } },
                            React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 800, color: compat.pct >= 70 ? C.green : compat.pct >= 40 ? C.amber : C.rose } }, compat.pct + "% compat\u00EDvel"),
                            React.createElement("div", { style: { flex: 1, height: 5, borderRadius: 3, background: C.line, overflow: "hidden" } },
                                React.createElement("div", { style: { height: "100%", width: compat.pct + "%", background: compat.pct >= 70 ? C.green : compat.pct >= 40 ? C.amber : C.rose, borderRadius: 3 } }))),

function BuscarCriadoresView(_a) {
    var ofertas = _a.ofertas, profile = _a.profile, plano = _a.plano, convidar = _a.convidar, notify = _a.notify;
    var _b = __read(React.useState([]), 2), criadores = _b[0], setCriadores = _b[1];
    var _c = __read(React.useState(false), 2), loading = _c[0], setLoading = _c[1];
    var _d = __read(React.useState(""), 2), busca = _d[0], setBusca = _d[1];
    var _e = __read(React.useState(0), 2), segMin = _e[0], setSegMin = _e[1];
    var _f = __read(React.useState(""), 2), nichoFiltro = _f[0], setNichoFiltro = _f[1];
    var _g = __read(React.useState(""), 2), convMsg = _g[0], setConvMsg = _g[1];
    var _h = __read(React.useState({}), 2), convSel = _h[0], setConvSel = _h[1];
    var brl = function (n) { return Number(n || 0).toLocaleString("pt-BR", { style: "currency", currency: "BRL" }); };
    useEffect(function () {
        var sb = window._sb;
        if (!sb)
            return;
        setLoading(true);
        sb.from("profiles").select("id, nome, nicho, plataformas, publico, handles, foto_url, plano, aceita_convites").eq("papel", "criador").not("nome", "is", null)
            .then(function (_a) {
            var data = _a.data;
            if (data)
                setCriadores(data.map(function (c) { return ({
                    id: c.id, nome: c.nome, nicho: c.nicho || "",
                    seguidores: Number((c.handles || {}).seguidores_num) || 0,
                    alcance: Number((c.handles || {}).alcance_num) || 0,
                    eng: Number((c.handles || {}).eng_num) || 0,
                    publico: c.publico || "", plataformas: c.plataformas || [],
                    foto: c.foto_url || "", pro: c.plano === "Pro",
                    handles: c.handles || {},
                    aceitaConvites: c.aceita_convites === false ? false : true,
                }); }));
            setLoading(false);
        });
    }, []);
    var _j = __read(React.useState(false), 2), criadoresFiltro = _j[0], setCriadoresFiltro = _j[1];
    var filtrados = criadores
        .filter(function (c) {
        if (busca) {
            var b = busca.toLowerCase().replace("@", "");
            var nome = (c.nome || "").toLowerCase();
            var nicho = (c.nicho || "").toLowerCase();
            var handlesStr = Object.keys(c.handles || {}).map(function (k) { return String((c.handles || {})[k] || "").toLowerCase(); }).join(" ");
            if (!nome.includes(b) && !nicho.includes(b) && !handlesStr.includes(b))
                return false;
        }
        if (nichoFiltro && c.nicho !== nichoFiltro)
            return false;
        if (Number(segMin) > 0 && c.seguidores < Number(segMin))
            return false;
        return true;
    })
        .sort(function (a, b) { return (b.pro ? 1 : 0) - (a.pro ? 1 : 0); });
    var nichos = __spreadArray([], __read(new Set(criadores.map(function (c) { return c.nicho; }).filter(Boolean))), false);
    function convidarCriador(cr, ofId) {
        if (!ofId)
            return;
        convidar(cr, ofId);
        setConvMsg("Convite enviado para " + cr.nome + "!");
        setTimeout(function () { return setConvMsg(""); }, 2500);
    }
    return (React.createElement("div", { style: { marginTop: 12 } },
        React.createElement(Sub, null, "Encontre criadores cadastrados e convide para suas campanhas."),
        React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", gap: 8, marginBottom: 12 } },
            React.createElement("input", { value: busca, onChange: function (e) { return setBusca(e.target.value); }, placeholder: "Buscar por nome, @ ou nicho...", style: { flex: 1, padding: "11px 14px", borderRadius: 11, border: "1px solid var(--line)", background: "var(--soft)", color: "var(--ink)", fontSize: 14, fontFamily: "'DM Sans',sans-serif", outline: "none" } }),
            React.createElement("button", { onClick: function () { return setCriadoresFiltro(function (o) { return !o; }); }, style: { padding: "11px 14px", borderRadius: 11, border: "1px solid ".concat((nichoFiltro || Number(segMin) > 0) ? "var(--accent)" : "var(--line)"), background: (nichoFiltro || Number(segMin) > 0) ? "rgba(179,102,255,.12)" : "transparent", cursor: "pointer", color: (nichoFiltro || Number(segMin) > 0) ? "var(--accent)" : "var(--mute)", fontWeight: 700, fontFamily: "'DM Sans',sans-serif", fontSize: 13, flexShrink: 0 } },
                "\u2699\uFE0F ",
                (nichoFiltro || Number(segMin) > 0) ? "Filtros ✓" : "Filtros")),
        criadoresFiltro && (React.createElement("div", { style: { borderRadius: 12, border: "1px solid var(--line)", background: "var(--card)", padding: 14, marginBottom: 12 } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { marginBottom: 12 } },
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 12, color: "var(--mute)", fontWeight: 600, marginBottom: 6 } }, "Nicho"),

    function publicar() {

function Tag(_a) {
    var children = _a.children;
    return React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 11.5, color: C.amber, background: "rgba(179,102,255,.1)", padding: "2px 8px", borderRadius: 6 } }, children);
}
function CarteiraScreen(_a) {
    var disponivel = _a.disponivel, pendente = _a.pendente, total = _a.total, sacado = _a.sacado, ganhoMarcas = _a.ganhoMarcas, ganhoProdutos = _a.ganhoProdutos, ganhoIndicacao = _a.ganhoIndicacao, emAnalise = _a.emAnalise, holdDias = _a.holdDias, onSacar = _a.onSacar, meusSaques = _a.meusSaques, movimentacoes = _a.movimentacoes, plano = _a.plano;
    var taxaSaque = plano === "Grátis" ? 3 : 0;

function ColabsScreen(_a) {
    var profile = _a.profile, colabs = _a.colabs, setColabs = _a.setColabs;
    var _busca = __read(React.useState(""), 2), busca = _busca[0], setBusca = _busca[1];
    var _pool = __read(React.useState([]), 2), poolReal = _pool[0], setPoolReal = _pool[1];
    var _load = __read(React.useState(true), 2), loading = _load[0], setLoading = _load[1];
    React.useEffect(function () {
        var sb = window._sb;
        if (!sb) { setLoading(false); return; }
        sb.from("profiles").select("id, nome, nicho, plataformas, handles, foto_url, seguidores, aceita_convites").eq("papel", "criador").not("nome", "is", null)
            .then(function (_a) {
            var data = _a.data;
            if (data) {
                var meu = (profile && profile.nome || "").toLowerCase();
                setPoolReal(data
                    .filter(function (c) { return (c.nome || "").toLowerCase() !== meu; })
                    .map(function (c) { return ({
                        nome: c.nome, nicho: c.nicho || "",
                        seguidores: c.seguidores || "",
                        plataformas: c.plataformas || [],
                        handles: c.handles || {},
                        foto: c.foto_url || "",
                        aceitaConvites: c.aceita_convites === false ? false : true,
                    }); }));
            }
            setLoading(false);
        });
    }, []);
    var nichoMatch = function (n) {
        var a = (n || "").toLowerCase().trim();
        var b = (profile.nicho || "").toLowerCase().trim();
        return !!a && !!b && (a.includes(b) || b.includes(a));
    };
    function enviarColab(cr, msg) {
        setColabs(function (arr) { return arr.some(function (c) { return c.com === cr.nome; }) ? arr : __spreadArray([{ id: Date.now(), com: cr.nome, nicho: cr.nicho, status: "enviado", mensagem: msg || "Bora colaborar?" }], __read(arr), false); });
    }
    function responderColab(id, aceitar) {
        setColabs(function (arr) { return arr.map(function (c) { return c.id === id ? __assign(__assign({}, c), { status: aceitar ? "aceito" : "recusado" }) : c; }); });
    }
    function mandarColab(id, text) {
        setColabs(function (arr) { return arr.map(function (c) { return c.id === id ? __assign(__assign({}, c), { msgs: __spreadArray(__spreadArray([], __read((c.msgs || [])), false), [{ from: "criador", text: text }], false) }) : c; }); });
        setTimeout(function () { return setColabs(function (arr) { return arr.map(function (c) {
            if (c.id !== id || (c.msgs || []).some(function (m) { return m.from === "parceiro"; }))
                return c;
            return __assign(__assign({}, c), { msgs: __spreadArray(__spreadArray([], __read((c.msgs || [])), false), [{ from: "parceiro", text: "Fechou! Bora marcar a gravação então 🎬" }], false) });
        }); }); }, 900);
    }
    var labelStatus = { recebido: { t: "Convite recebido", cor: C.amber }, enviado: { t: "Aguardando resposta", cor: C.mute }, aceito: { t: "✅ Colab ativa", cor: C.green }, recusado: { t: "Recusado", cor: C.rose } };
    var poolFiltrado = poolReal.filter(function (c) {
        if (!busca) return true;
        var b = busca.toLowerCase().replace("@", "");
        var nome = (c.nome || "").toLowerCase();
        var nicho = (c.nicho || "").toLowerCase();
        var handlesStr = Object.keys(c.handles || {}).map(function (k) { return String((c.handles || {})[k] || "").toLowerCase(); }).join(" ");
        return nome.includes(b) || nicho.includes(b) || handlesStr.includes(b);
    });
    return (React.createElement("div", { className: "rise" },
        React.createElement("h2", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 24, margin: "16px 0 2px", fontWeight: 700 } }, "Colabs"),

function FerramentasScreen(_a) {
    var perfilTexto = _a.perfilTexto, plano = _a.plano, onVoltar = _a.onVoltar;
    var _b = __read(React.useState(null), 2), ferramenta = _b[0], setFerramenta = _b[1];
    var _c = __read(React.useState(""), 2), entrada = _c[0], setEntrada = _c[1];
    var _d = __read(React.useState(""), 2), resultado = _d[0], setResultado = _d[1];
    var _e = __read(React.useState(false), 2), carregando = _e[0], setCarregando = _e[1];
    var _f = __read(React.useState(""), 2), erro = _f[0], setErro = _f[1];
    var _g = __read(React.useState(false), 2), copiado = _g[0], setCopiado = _g[1];
    var LIMITE_DIA = plano === "Pro" ? 30 : plano === "Criador" ? 20 : 0;
    function chaveHoje() {
        var d = new Date();
        return "cria_ferr_" + d.getFullYear() + "-" + (d.getMonth() + 1) + "-" + d.getDate();
    }
    function usosHoje() {
        try {
            return parseInt(localStorage.getItem(chaveHoje()) || "0", 10) || 0;
        }

    return (React.createElement("div", { style: { marginTop: 8 } },
        React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", gap: 6, marginBottom: 16 } }, [1, 2, 3].map(function (n) {
            return React.createElement("div", { key: n, style: { flex: 1, height: 5, borderRadius: 3, background: n <= etapa ? "linear-gradient(135deg,".concat(C.amber, ",").concat(C.rose, ")") : C.line } });
        })),
        React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 12, color: C.amber, fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: 1, textTransform: "uppercase", marginBottom: 4 } }, "Passo ".concat(etapa, " de ").concat(TOTAL)),
        React.createElement("h3", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 700, margin: "0 0 12px" } }, titulos[etapa - 1]),
        etapa === 1 ? bloco1 : etapa === 2 ? bloco2 : bloco3,
        ((etapa < TOTAL && !podeAvancar) || (etapa === TOTAL && !ok)) && faltando.length > 0 && React.createElement("div", { style: { marginTop: 16, padding: "11px 14px", borderRadius: 11, background: "rgba(255,77,141,.1)", border: "1px solid rgba(255,77,141,.3)", fontSize: 12.5, color: C.rose, lineHeight: 1.5 } }, "Pra continuar, falta preencher: " + faltando.join(", ") + "."),
        React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", gap: 10, marginTop: 22 } },
            etapa > 1 && React.createElement("button", { onClick: function () { return setEtapa(etapa - 1); }, style: { flex: "0 0 auto", padding: "14px 20px", borderRadius: 12, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: "transparent", color: C.ink, fontFamily: "'DM Sans',sans-serif", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: 14.5, cursor: "pointer" } }, "\u2039 Voltar"),
            etapa < TOTAL ? React.createElement("button", { onClick: function () { if (podeAvancar) setEtapa(etapa + 1); }, disabled: !podeAvancar, style: { flex: 1, padding: "14px", borderRadius: 12, border: "none", cursor: podeAvancar ? "pointer" : "default", fontFamily: "'DM Sans',sans-serif", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: 15, background: podeAvancar ? "linear-gradient(135deg,".concat(C.amber, ",").concat(C.rose, ")") : C.line, color: podeAvancar ? "var(--onAccent)" : C.mute } }, "Pr\u00F3ximo \u203A") : React.createElement("button", { onClick: function () { if (ok) onSave(d); }, disabled: !ok, style: { flex: 1, padding: "14px", borderRadius: 12, border: "none", cursor: ok ? "pointer" : "default", fontFamily: "'DM Sans',sans-serif", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: 15, background: ok ? "linear-gradient(135deg,".concat(C.amber, ",").concat(C.rose, ")") : C.line, color: ok ? "var(--onAccent)" : C.mute } }, "\u26A1 Começar"))));
}

var Sub = function (_a) {

function BarChart(_a) {
    var data = _a.data;
    if (!data || !data.length)
        return null;
    var max = Math.max.apply(Math, __spreadArray([1], __read(data.map(function (d) { return d.value; })), false));
    var W = 300, H = 140, padX = 14, padB = 26, padT = 16;
    var bw = (W - padX * 2) / data.length;
    return (React.createElement("svg", { viewBox: "0 0 ".concat(W, " ").concat(H), width: "100%", style: { display: "block" } },
        React.createElement("defs", null,
            React.createElement("linearGradient", { id: "barGrad", x1: "0", y1: "0", x2: "0", y2: "1" },
                React.createElement("stop", { offset: "0", stopColor: "var(--accent)" }),
                React.createElement("stop", { offset: "1", stopColor: "var(--rose)" }))),
        React.createElement("line", { x1: padX, y1: H - padB, x2: W - padX, y2: H - padB, stroke: "var(--line)", strokeWidth: "1" }),
        data.map(function (d, i) {
            var h = (d.value / max) * (H - padB - padT);
            var w = Math.min(34, bw * 0.6);
            var x = padX + i * bw + (bw - w) / 2;
            var y = H - padB - h;
            return (React.createElement("g", { key: i },
                React.createElement("rect", { x: x, y: y, width: w, height: Math.max(h, 1), rx: "5", fill: "url(#barGrad)" }),
                React.createElement("text", { x: x + w / 2, y: y - 4, textAnchor: "middle", fontSize: "9.5", fontWeight: "700", fill: "var(--ink)" }, d.value),
                React.createElement("text", { x: x + w / 2, y: H - 9, textAnchor: "middle", fontSize: "8.5", fill: "var(--mute)" }, d.label)));
        })));
}
function DashboardScreen(_a) {
    var profile = _a.profile, plano = _a.plano, usosSemana = _a.usosSemana, limiteSemana = _a.limiteSemana, ganhoMarcas = _a.ganhoMarcas, ganhoProdutos = _a.ganhoProdutos, ganhoIndicacao = _a.ganhoIndicacao, totalGanho = _a.totalGanho, sacado = _a.sacado, ganhoPendente = _a.ganhoPendente, ofertas = _a.ofertas, vendas = _a.vendas, colabs = _a.colabs, arquivados = _a.arquivados, produtos = _a.produtos, onIr = _a.onIr;
    var brl = function (n) { return Number(n || 0).toLocaleString("pt-BR", { style: "currency", currency: "BRL" }); };
    var meuNome = profile.nome || "Criador";
    var disponivel = totalGanho - sacado;
    var dias7 = ["Dom", "Seg", "Ter", "Qua", "Qui", "Sex", "Sáb"];
    var hoje = new Date().getDay();
    var semana = __spreadArray([], __read(Array(7)), false).map(function (_, i) { return dias7[(hoje - 6 + i + 7) % 7]; });
    var seed = Math.abs(totalGanho * 100) || 0;
    var tendencia = semana.map(function (lb, i) {
        var frac = (i + 1) / 7;
        var ruido = seed > 0 ? Math.sin(seed * (i + 1) * 0.3) * totalGanho * 0.08 : 0;
        return { label: lb, value: Math.max(0, parseFloat((totalGanho * frac * 0.6 + ruido).toFixed(2))) };
    });
    tendencia[6] = { label: semana[6], value: parseFloat(totalGanho.toFixed(2)) };
    var meusProd = (produtos || []).filter(function (p) { return p.dono === meuNome || (vendas || []).some(function (v) { return v.afiliado === meuNome && v.produtoId === p.id; }); });
    var vendasDe = function (pid) { return (vendas || []).filter(function (v) { return v.produtoId === pid; }).length; };
    var minhasCands = (ofertas || []).flatMap(function (of) { return (of.candidatos || []).filter(function (c) { return c.nome === meuNome; }).map(function (c) { return (__assign(__assign({}, c), { titulo: of.titulo })); }); });
    var nAbertas = minhasCands.filter(function (c) { return c.status === "aprovado"; }).length;
    var nConcluidas = minhasCands.filter(function (c) { return c.status === "concluido"; }).length;
    var nColabAtivas = (colabs || []).filter(function (c) { return c.status === "aceito"; }).length;
    var nArquivados = (arquivados || []).length;
    var recente = __spreadArray(__spreadArray(__spreadArray([], __read((vendas || []).slice(0, 3).map(function (v) { return ({ tipo: "venda", texto: "Venda: ".concat(v.nome), valor: v.preco * (1 - 0.05) * (v.afiliado === meuNome ? v.comissao / 100 : 1 - v.comissao / 100) }); })), false), __read(minhasCands.filter(function (c) { return c.status === "concluido"; }).slice(0, 2).map(function (c) { return ({ tipo: "campanha", texto: "Campanha paga: ".concat(c.titulo), valor: null }); })), false), __read((colabs || []).filter(function (c) { return c.status === "aceito"; }).slice(0, 2).map(function (c) { return ({ tipo: "colab", texto: "Colab ativa: ".concat(c.parceiro), valor: null }); })), false).slice(0, 5);
    var iconeTipo = { venda: "🛒", campanha: "🤝", colab: "🎬" };
    return (React.createElement("div", { className: "rise", style: { paddingBottom: 24 } },
        React.createElement("div", { style: { marginBottom: 18 } },
            React.createElement("h2", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 22, fontWeight: 800, margin: "16px 0 2px" } },
                "Boa, ",
                meuNome.split(" ")[0],
                "! \uD83D\uDC4B"),
            React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 13.5, color: C.mute, margin: 0 } },
                "Esta semana: ",
                React.createElement("strong", { style: { color: usosSemana >= limiteSemana ? C.rose : C.green } },
                    usosSemana,
                    "/",

                " pautas geradas \u00B7 plano ",
                React.createElement("strong", { style: { color: C.amber } }, plano))),

            { lb: "Disponível", v: disponivel, cor: C.green },
            { lb: "A receber", v: ganhoPendente, cor: C.amber },

        ].map(function (_a) {
            var lb = _a.lb, v = _a.v, cor = _a.cor;
            return (React.createElement("div", { key: lb, style: { borderRadius: 13, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: C.card, padding: "13px 14px" } },
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 11, color: C.mute, textTransform: "uppercase", letterSpacing: 1 } }, lb),

                        iconeTipo[a.tipo] || "•",
                        " ",
                        React.createElement("span", { style: { color: C.ink } }, a.texto)),
                    a.valor != null && React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: C.green, flexShrink: 0, marginLeft: 8 } },
                        "+",
                        brl(a.valor)))); }))));
}
function LineChart(_a) {
    var data = _a.data, _b = _a.cor, cor = _b === void 0 ? "var(--accent)" : _b;
    if (!data || data.length < 2)
        return null;
    var W = 300, H = 100, padX = 10, padB = 20, padT = 12;
    var max = Math.max.apply(Math, __spreadArray([1], __read(data.map(function (d) { return d.value; })), false));
    var xs = data.map(function (_, i) { return padX + (i / (data.length - 1)) * (W - padX * 2); });
    var ys = data.map(function (d) { return H - padB - (d.value / max) * (H - padB - padT); });
    var path = xs.map(function (x, i) { return "".concat(i === 0 ? "M" : "L").concat(x.toFixed(1), ",").concat(ys[i].toFixed(1)); }).join(" ");
    var area = "".concat(path, " L").concat(xs[xs.length - 1].toFixed(1), ",").concat(H - padB, " L").concat(xs[0].toFixed(1), ",").concat(H - padB, " Z");
    return (React.createElement("svg", { viewBox: "0 0 ".concat(W, " ").concat(H), width: "100%", style: { display: "block" } },
        React.createElement("defs", null,
            React.createElement("linearGradient", { id: "areaGrad", x1: "0", y1: "0", x2: "0", y2: "1" },
                React.createElement("stop", { offset: "0", stopColor: cor, stopOpacity: "0.25" }),
                React.createElement("stop", { offset: "1", stopColor: cor, stopOpacity: "0" }))),
        React.createElement("path", { d: area, fill: "url(#areaGrad)" }),
        React.createElement("path", { d: path, fill: "none", stroke: cor, strokeWidth: "2.2", strokeLinejoin: "round", strokeLinecap: "round" }),
        data.map(function (d, i) { return (React.createElement("g", { key: i },
            React.createElement("circle", { cx: xs[i], cy: ys[i], r: "3.2", fill: cor }),
            React.createElement("text", { x: xs[i], y: H - 5, textAnchor: "middle", fontSize: "8", fill: "var(--mute)" }, d.label))); })));
}
function BloqueioPlano(_a) {
    var titulo = _a.titulo, sub = _a.sub, onIr = _a.onIr;
    return (React.createElement("div", { className: "rise", style: { textAlign: "center", padding: "48px 22px" } },
        React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 40 } }, "\uD83D\uDD12"),

        React.createElement(Botao, { onClick: onIr, style: { maxWidth: 220, margin: "0 auto" } }, "Ver planos")));
}
var Label = function (_a) {
    var children = _a.children;
    return React.createElement("label", { style: { display: "block", fontSize: 12.5, fontWeight: 600, color: C.mute, margin: "16px 0 7px" } }, children);
};
var Rot = function (_a) {
    var children = _a.children;
    return React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 11, letterSpacing: 1.5, color: C.mute, textTransform: "uppercase" } }, children);
};
function Input(_a) {
    var value = _a.value, onChange = _a.onChange, placeholder = _a.placeholder;
    return React.createElement("input", { value: value, onChange: function (e) { return onChange(e.target.value); }, placeholder: placeholder, style: { width: "100%", padding: "13px 14px", borderRadius: 11, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: C.soft, color: C.ink, fontSize: 14.5, fontFamily: "'DM Sans', sans-serif", outline: "none" } });
}
function FotoUpload(_a) {
    var value = _a.value, onChange = _a.onChange, _b = _a.size, size = _b === void 0 ? 76 : _b, redondo = _a.redondo, _c = _a.rotulo, rotulo = _c === void 0 ? "Adicionar foto" : _c;
    var _d = __read(React.useState(false), 2), enviando = _d[0], setEnviando = _d[1];
    var onFile = function (e) {
        var f = e.target.files && e.target.files[0];
        if (!f)
            return;
        var sb = window._sb;
        if (!sb || !sb.storage) {
            var r = new FileReader();
            r.onload = function () { return onChange(r.result); };
            r.readAsDataURL(f);
            return;
        }
        setEnviando(true);
        var ext = (f.name && f.name.indexOf(".") >= 0) ? f.name.split(".").pop() : "jpg";
        var caminho = "img_" + Date.now() + "_" + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8) + "." + ext;
        sb.storage.from("imagens").upload(caminho, f, { cacheControl: "3600", upsert: true }).then(function (res) {
            if (res.error) {
                setEnviando(false);
                try { toastErro("Erro ao enviar imagem: " + res.error.message); } catch (ee) { }
                return;
            }
            var pub = sb.storage.from("imagens").getPublicUrl(caminho);
            var url = pub && pub.data && pub.data.publicUrl;
            setEnviando(false);
            if (url)
                onChange(url);
        }).catch(function (err) {
            setEnviando(false);
            try { toastErro("Erro ao enviar imagem: " + (err && err.message ? err.message : err)); } catch (ee) { }
        });
    };
    return (React.createElement("label", { style: { display: "inline-flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, cursor: "pointer" } },
        React.createElement("span", { style: { width: size, height: size, borderRadius: redondo ? "50%" : 14, overflow: "hidden", border: "1px dashed ".concat(C.line), background: C.soft, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 } }, enviando ? React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 11, color: C.amber } }, "...") : value ? React.createElement("img", { src: value, alt: "", style: { width: "100%", height: "100%", objectFit: "cover" } }) : React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 22, color: C.mute } }, "\uFF0B")),
        React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 13, color: C.amber, fontWeight: 600 } }, enviando ? "Enviando..." : value ? "Trocar foto" : rotulo),
        React.createElement("input", { type: "file", accept: "image/*", onChange: onFile, style: { display: "none" } })));
}
function NumberField(_a) {
    var value = _a.value, onChange = _a.onChange, placeholder = _a.placeholder;
    return (React.createElement("div", { style: { flex: 1, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", background: C.soft, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), borderRadius: 11, padding: "0 10px" } },
        React.createElement("input", { type: "number", inputMode: "numeric", value: value || "", onChange: function (e) { return onChange(e.target.value); }, placeholder: placeholder, style: { width: "100%", padding: "13px 0", background: "transparent", border: "none", color: C.ink, fontSize: 14, outline: "none", fontFamily: "'DM Sans', sans-serif" } })));
}
function Chips(_a) {
    var options = _a.options, value = _a.value, onChange = _a.onChange, multi = _a.multi;
    var toggle = function (o) {
        if (!multi)
            return onChange(o);
        onChange(value.includes(o) ? value.filter(function (x) { return x !== o; }) : __spreadArray(__spreadArray([], __read(value), false), [o], false));
    };
    return (React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", flexWrap: "wrap", gap: 8 } }, options.map(function (o) {
        var on = multi ? value.includes(o) : value === o;
        return (React.createElement("button", { key: o, onClick: function () { return toggle(o); }, style: {
                padding: "9px 14px", borderRadius: 11, cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 13.5, fontWeight: 600, fontFamily: "'DM Sans', sans-serif", transition: "all .15s",
                border: "1px solid ".concat(on ? C.amber : C.line),
                background: on ? "linear-gradient(135deg, ".concat(C.amber, ", ").concat(C.amberDeep, ")") : "transparent",
                color: on ? "var(--onAccent)" : C.ink,
            } }, o));
    })));
}
function Botao(_a) {
    var children = _a.children, onClick = _a.onClick, disabled = _a.disabled, style = _a.style, variante = _a.variante, tamanho = _a.tamanho, full = _a.full;
    // Variantes de estilo. Padr\u00E3o = "primario" (mant\u00E9m comportamento antigo).
    var v = variante || "primario";
    var larguraTotal = full !== false; // por padr\u00E3o full-width, como era antes
    var pad = tamanho === "sm" ? "9px 14px" : tamanho === "lg" ? "16px 22px" : "14px 18px";
    var fSize = tamanho === "sm" ? DS.fs.sm : tamanho === "lg" ? DS.fs.lg : 15;
    var base = { width: larguraTotal ? "100%" : "auto", padding: pad, borderRadius: DS.r.md, border: "none", cursor: disabled ? "default" : "pointer", fontFamily: DS.ff.body, fontSize: fSize, fontWeight: DS.fw.bold, transition: "opacity .2s, transform .1s", opacity: disabled ? 0.7 : 1 };
    var estilos = {
        primario: { background: disabled ? C.line : "linear-gradient(135deg, ".concat(C.amber, ", ").concat(C.amberDeep, ")"), color: disabled ? C.mute : C.onAccent, boxShadow: disabled ? "none" : DS.sh.glow },
        secundario: { background: C.soft, color: C.ink, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line) },
        fantasma: { background: "transparent", color: C.amber, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line) },
        perigo: { background: "transparent", color: C.rose, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.rose) },
    };
    return (React.createElement("button", { onClick: onClick, disabled: disabled, style: __assign(__assign(__assign({}, base), estilos[v] || estilos.primario), style || {}) }, children));
}

        React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 40, marginBottom: DS.sp.md, opacity: .9 } }, emoji || "\u2728"),
        titulo && React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: DS.fs.lg, fontWeight: DS.fw.bold, color: C.ink, marginBottom: DS.sp.xs } }, titulo),
        texto && React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: DS.fs.md, color: C.mute, lineHeight: 1.55, maxWidth: 300, margin: "0 auto" } }, texto),
        acao && React.createElement("div", { style: { marginTop: DS.sp.lg, display: "flex", justifyContent: "center" } }, acao));
}
// Skeleton: bloco de carregamento com brilho. D\u00E1 sensa\u00E7\u00E3o de velocidade.
// Uso: React.createElement(Skeleton, { h: 20, w: "80%" })
function Skeleton(_a) {
    var h = _a.h, w = _a.w, r = _a.r, mb = _a.mb;
    return React.createElement("div", { style: { height: h || 16, width: w || "100%", borderRadius: r || DS.r.sm, background: "linear-gradient(90deg, ".concat(C.soft, " 25%, ").concat(C.line, " 50%, ").concat(C.soft, " 75%)"), backgroundSize: "200% 100%", animation: "shimmer 1.4s ease infinite", marginBottom: mb === undefined ? DS.sp.sm : mb } });
}
function Bloco(_a) {
    var rotulo = _a.rotulo, texto = _a.texto, cor = _a.cor;
    if (!texto)
        return null;
    return React.createElement("div", { style: { marginTop: 10 } },
        React.createElement(Rot, null, rotulo),
        React.createElement("p", { style: { margin: "4px 0 0", fontSize: 14, lineHeight: 1.5, color: cor || C.ink } }, texto));
}

// =============================================================
// ErrorBoundary — rede de segurança contra "tela preta".
// Captura qualquer erro de renderização dentro do app e mostra
// uma tela amigável em vez de desmontar tudo.
// Precisa ser class component (única exceção que o React exige).
// =============================================================
function ErrorBoundary(props) {
    React.Component.call(this, props);
    this.state = { erro: null };
}
ErrorBoundary.prototype = Object.create(React.Component.prototype);
ErrorBoundary.prototype.constructor = ErrorBoundary;
ErrorBoundary.getDerivedStateFromError = function (erro) {
    return { erro: erro };
};
ErrorBoundary.prototype.componentDidCatch = function (erro, info) {
    // Log leve para depuração (sem dados pessoais)
    try {
        console.error("[Cria] Erro capturado pelo ErrorBoundary:", erro && erro.message, info && info.componentStack);
    } catch (e) { }
};
ErrorBoundary.prototype.render = function () {
    if (this.state.erro) {
        return React.createElement("div", { style: { minHeight: "100vh", display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", padding: 28, background: "var(--bg)", textAlign: "center", fontFamily: "'DM Sans', sans-serif" } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 44, marginBottom: 14 } }, "\uD83D\uDEE0\uFE0F"),
            React.createElement("h2", { style: { fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 800, color: "var(--ink)", margin: "0 0 8px" } }, "Algo travou por aqui"),
            React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 14, color: "var(--mute)", lineHeight: 1.55, margin: "0 0 22px", maxWidth: 320 } }, "Tivemos um probleminha inesperado nesta tela. Seus dados est\u00E3o salvos \u2014 \u00E9 s\u00F3 recarregar que tudo volta ao normal."),
            React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 11, color: "#ff8080", background: "rgba(255,90,110,.1)", border: "1px solid rgba(255,90,110,.3)", borderRadius: 8, padding: "10px 12px", margin: "0 0 18px", maxWidth: 340, wordBreak: "break-word", fontFamily: "monospace", textAlign: "left" } }, "Detalhe t\u00E9cnico: " + String((this.state.erro && this.state.erro.message) || this.state.erro || "desconhecido")),
            React.createElement("button", { onClick: function () { try { window.location.reload(); } catch (e) { } }, style: { padding: "13px 28px", borderRadius: 13, border: "none", background: "linear-gradient(135deg, var(--accent), var(--rose))", color: "#fff", fontFamily: "'DM Sans', sans-serif", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: 15, cursor: "pointer" } }, "Recarregar o app"));
    }
    return this.props.children;
};

ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById("root")).render(React.createElement(ErrorBoundary, null, React.createElement(React.Fragment, null, React.createElement(App, null), React.createElement(ToastHost, null))));document.getElementById("boot").style.display="none";
